<span data-ttu-id="93315-1148">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2003 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93315-1148">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2003 R2:</span></span>
